cs.bgra : cs;\n  vec4 cmixed = mix(c, cs, mixer);\n  vec4 soft = vec4(c);\n  vec3 ck = cs.rgb - black.rgb;\n  float vc = variance(ck.r * factors.r, ck.g * factors.g, ck.b * factors.b);\n  c.rb = rbsoftsoft + (sharpen * vec2(lapG));\n  c.g = cmixed.g;\n  c.rb = mix(cmixed.rb, c.rb, min(1.0, cardinalMixing * cardinalInstability));\n  if (vc < (1e-4 * minVarNeutral)) {\n    vec2 drb = abs(cs.rb - soft.rb);\n    c.r = mix(c.r, cmixed.r, min(1.0, (drb.x * varNeutralMixer) / (vc + eps)));\n    c.b = mix(c.b, cmixed.b, min(1.0, (drb.y * varNeutralMixer) / (vc + eps)));\n  }\n  if (isHF) c.rb = cmixed.rb;\n  c.rgb = max(c.rgb - black.rgb, 0.0);\n  c.rgb *= range;\n  c.rgb = min(c.rgb, 1.0);\n  vec4 x = clamp(vec4(destCoord(), crop.zw - destCoord()) + 0.5, 0.0, 1.0);\n  c *= ((x.x * x.y) * x.z) * x.w;\n  return c;\n}\n"
- "kernel vec4 _planarToInterleaved3(sampler s, float tileSize) {\n  vec2 dc = destCoord();\n  if ((((dc.x < 0.0) || (dc.x > tileSize)) || (dc.y < 0.0)) || (dc.y > tileSize)) return vec4(0.0);\n  dc.y = clamp(dc.y, 0.0, tileSize);\n  vec4 rgba = vec4(1.0);\n  vec2 delta = vec2(0.0, tileSize);\n  rgba.r = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 2.0))).x;\n  rgba.g = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 1.0))).x;\n  rgba.b = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 0.0))).x;\n  return rgba;\n}\n"
- "kernel vec4 _planarToInterleaved4(sampler s, float tileSize) {\n  vec2 dc = destCoord();\n  if ((((dc.x < 0.0) || (dc.x > tileSize)) || (dc.y < 0.0)) || (dc.y > tileSize)) return vec4(0.0);\n  dc.y = clamp(dc.y, 0.0, tileSize);\n  vec4 rgba = vec4(1.0);\n  vec2 delta = vec2(0.0, tileSize);\n  rgba.r = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 3.0))).x;\n  rgba.g = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 2.0))).x;\n  rgba.b = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 1.0))).x;\n  rgba.a = sample(s, samplerTransform(s, dc + (delta * 0.0))).x;\n  return rgba;\n}\n"
